	<h2 class="feed-title">Now</h2><!--set: now_item_757307879718916883_false_desktop_2018-02-19T18:31:08Z_2018-02-19T18:31:08Z_true_11--><article data-id="757307879718916883" data-time="1519065068000" class="now-feed-item now-feed-shortstop has-media module_bloom_behavior  no-thumb thumb" data-behavior=" module_bloom" data-sport="46" data-teams="14"><div class="now-content bloom-content"><h1>Fang Yuan <span>&nbsp;</span></h1><div class="img-container" data-main-container=".now-feed-item"><img class="focus-image  lazyloaded" data-lazyload="true" data-src="http://a.espncdn.com/photo/2016/0923/r130102_130x180_smallmug.jpg" src="http://a.espncdn.com/photo/2016/0923/r130102_130x180_smallmug.jpg"></div><p>A closer look at the Li Ning Way of Wade 6 "Moment" which released on Li Ning's commercial event during the ASW at LA.
